per_route) {\n  // Copy request headers from config\n  for (const auto& header : config.request_headers()) {\n    request_headers_.push_back(header);\n  }\n\n  // Copy response headers from config\n  for (const auto& header : config.response_headers()) {\n    response_headers_.push_back(header);\n  }\n\n  // For per-route config, ensure at least one header injection rule is specified\n  if (per_route && request_headers_.empty() && response_headers_.empty()) {\n    throw EnvoyException(\"custom_header_injection_filter: Per route filter config must specify \"\n                         \"either request_headers or response_headers\");\n  }\n}\n\nCustomHeaderInjectionFilter::CustomHeaderInjectionFilter(const ConfigSharedPtr config)\n    : config_(config) {}\n\nCustomHeaderInjectionFilter::~CustomHeaderInjectionFilter() = default;\n\nHttp::FilterHeadersStatus CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::decodeHeaders(\n    Http::RequestHeaderMap& headers, bool) {\n  const auto* config = getConfig();\n  const auto& request_headers = config->requestHeaders();\n\n  if (!request_headers.empty()) {\n    injectHeaders(headers, request_headers);\n  }\n\n  return Http::FilterHeadersStatus::Continue;\n}\n\nvoid CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::setDecoderFilterCallbacks(\n    Http::StreamDecoderFilterCallbacks& callbacks) {\n  decoder_callbacks_ = &callbacks;\n}\n\nHttp::FilterHeadersStatus CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::encodeHeaders(\n    Http::ResponseHeaderMap& headers, bool) {\n  const auto* config = getConfig();\n  const auto& response_headers = config->responseHeaders();\n\n  if (!response_headers.empty()) {\n    injectHeaders(headers, response_headers);\n  }\n\n  return Http::FilterHeadersStatus::Continue;\n}\n\nvoid CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::setEncoderFilterCallbacks(\n    Http::StreamEncoderFilterCallbacks& callbacks) {\n  encoder_callbacks_ = &callbacks;\n}\n\nvoid CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::injectHeaders(\n    Http::HeaderMap& headers, const std::vector<ProtoHeaderInjection>& injections) {\n  for (const auto& injection : injections) {\n    Http::LowerCaseString header_name(injection.header_name());\n    headers.setCopy(header_name, injection.header_value());\n  }\n}\n\nconst Config* CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::getConfig() const {\n  // Cached config pointer.\n  if (effective_config_) {\n    return effective_config_;\n  }\n\n  effective_config_ =\n      Http::Utility::resolveMostSpecificPerFilterConfig<Config>(decoder_callbacks_);\n  if (effective_config_) {\n    return effective_config_;\n  }\n\n  effective_config_ = config_.get();\n  return effective_config_;\n}\n\n} // namespace CustomHeaderInjectionFilter\n} // namespace HttpFilters\n} // namespace Extensions\n} // namespace Envoy\n","numLines":97,"startLine":1,"totalLines":97}}}
